window.deltaScrollConfig = {
thresholds: [100, 300],
buffer: 0,
scrollWait: 50,
initialScroll: null,
scrollEventCount: 0,
thresholdsReached: {}
};

window.debounce = function(func, wait) {
let timeout;
return function(...args) {
clearTimeout(timeout);
timeout = setTimeout(() => func.apply(this, args), wait);
};
}

window.debouncedScrollEvent = null;

function trackScrollEvent() {
const config = window.deltaScrollConfig;
if (config.scrollEventCount < config.buffer) {
config.scrollEventCount += 1;
return;
}

const currentScroll = window.scrollY;

// Check if initialScroll is null to set it the first time so we only set it when it hasn't been initialized yet
// Using null avoids false positives from valid scroll positions like 0
if (config.initialScroll === null) {
config.initialScroll = currentScroll;
} else {
const delta = Math.abs(currentScroll - config.initialScroll);

config.thresholds.forEach((threshold) => {
if (delta >= threshold && !config.thresholdsReached[threshold]) {
window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
// This keeps original naming for the 300px threshold since it is already in use.
// @todo: Remove the following conditional once GTM is updated with new name.
if (threshold === 300) {
window.dataLayer.push({ event: 'user_scrolled_delta' });
}
window.dataLayer.push({
event: 'user_scrolled_delta_' + threshold + 'px',
threshold: threshold
});
config.thresholdsReached[threshold] = true;
// Update initialScroll after firing an event to reset the delta calculation for the next threshold
config.initialScroll = currentScroll;
}
});
}

if (Object.keys(config.thresholdsReached).length === config.thresholds.length) {
window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.debouncedScrollEvent);
}
}

// @see https://support.blueconic.com/hc/en-us/articles/202605221-JavaScript-front-end-API#h_01HD28B475743B4021J1AQ0CTN
function handleBlueConicLoad() {
window.removeEventListener('onBlueConicLoaded', handleBlueConicLoad, false);
window.debouncedScrollEvent = window.debounce(trackScrollEvent, window.deltaScrollConfig.scrollWait);
window.addEventListener('scroll', window.debouncedScrollEvent, { passive: true });
}

window.addEventListener('onBlueConicLoaded', handleBlueConicLoad, false);

function getDeviceType() {
const userAgent = navigator.userAgent;
if (/iPad|Tablet|PlayBook|Kindle|Silk/i.test(userAgent)) return "tablet";
if (/Mobi|Android|iPhone|Windows Phone|webOS/i.test(userAgent)) return "mobile";
return "desktop";
}

function getUserStatus(interval = 100, timeout = 1000) {
console.debug("ðŸ”¹ Checking subscriber status...");
return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
const startTime = Date.now();

const poll = setInterval(() => {
if (typeof window.subscriber === "undefined" || typeof window.keyValues === "undefined") {
return; // Ensure window.subscriber and window.keyValues exist
}

const isSubscriber = Boolean(window.subscriber); // True if subscribed, False otherwise
const isLoggedIn = Boolean(window.keyValues?.dnLoggedIn); // True if logged in

let result = {
status: 0, // Default: Anonymous user
type: "anonymous"
};

if (isSubscriber) {
result = { status: 2, type: "subscribed" };
} else if (!isSubscriber && isLoggedIn) {
result = { status: 1, type: "registered" };
}

clearInterval(poll);
console.debug("ðŸ“Œ Subscriber status:", result.status, "(", result.type, ")");
resolve(result);

if (Date.now() - startTime > timeout) {
clearInterval(poll);
reject(new Error("Timeout: subscriber status not found."));
}
}, interval);
});
}

function shouldOverrideByRule() {
if (typeof window === "undefined") return 0;
console.debug("ðŸ”¹ Checking paywall override conditions...");
// Load rules from JSON
const {
excludeTags,
excludeSections,
includeHostName,
externalDomain,
excludeURLPaths,
excludeHostName,
includeTags,
includeSections,
includePaths,
publishedDurationThreshold
} = {"excludeTags":["abode","timeless-in-texas"],"excludeSections":["/abode/","/arts-entertainment/things-to-do/","/branded-content/","/checkout/","/classifieds/","/custom-embed/","/espanol/","/help/","/login/","/marketplace/","/offers/","/opinion/send-a-letter/","/parks-guide/","/partner/","/pay-join-checkout/","/pay-join-receipt/","/query-by-tag-date/","/single-page-checkout/","/sports/sports-scrape/","/sponsored/","/subscribe/","/timeless-in-texas/","/top-workplaces-dfw/"],"includeHostName":["staging.dallasnews.com","dallasnews.com","localhost"],"excludeHostName":["dmn.arcpublishing.com","sandbox.dmn.arcpublishing.com"],"excludeURLPaths":["/best-in-dfw/","/care-facility/","/fwddfw/","/interactives/","/event/","/organization/","/organizations/","/person/","/place/","/school/","/custom-embed/"],"includeTags":[],"includeSections":["/voter-guide/","/high-school-sports/","/opinion/editorials/"],"includePaths":["/high-school-sports/"],"publishedDurationThreshold":28};

// Convert arrays into Sets for fast lookup
const EXCLUDE_TAGS = new Set(excludeTags);
const EXCLUDE_SECTIONS = new Set(excludeSections);
const EXCLUDE_PATHS = new Set(excludeURLPaths);
const EXCLUDE_HOST = new Set(excludeHostName);
const INCLUDE_HOST = new Set(includeHostName);
const INCLUDE_TAGS = new Set(includeTags);
const INCLUDE_SECTIONS = new Set(includeSections);
const INCLUDE_PATHS = new Set(includePaths);

console.debug("ðŸªµ Loaded Paywall Rules:", { EXCLUDE_TAGS, EXCLUDE_SECTIONS, EXCLUDE_PATHS, EXCLUDE_HOST, INCLUDE_TAGS, INCLUDE_SECTIONS, INCLUDE_PATHS, PUBLISHED_DURATION_THRESHOLD: publishedDurationThreshold});

// **Extract Key Values from Window Object**
const { location, contentRestrictions = "normal", keyValues = {} } = window;
const currentURL = location.href;
const isLockedByContentRestriction = contentRestrictions === "locked";
const isUnlockedByContentRestriction = contentRestrictions === "unlocked";
const tags = keyValues.tags?.map(tag => tag.toLowerCase()) || [];
const sectionId = (keyValues.sectionId || "").replace(/\/?$/, "/");
const publishedDuration = keyValues.publishedDuration || 0;

console.debug("ðŸªµ Paywall Decision Input:", { currentURL, isLockedByContentRestriction, tags, sectionId, publishedDuration });

// **Helper Functions**
const matchesTag = (tagSet) => tags.some(tag => tagSet.has(tag));
const matchesSection = (sectionSet) => [...sectionSet].some(excluded => sectionId.startsWith(excluded));
const matchesPath = (pathSet) => [...pathSet].some(path => location.pathname.startsWith(path));
const matchesHost = (hostSet) => hostSet.has(location.hostname);

// **Determine if URL is excluded**
const isExcluded = matchesTag(EXCLUDE_TAGS) ||
matchesSection(EXCLUDE_SECTIONS) ||
(matchesPath(EXCLUDE_PATHS) && matchesHost(INCLUDE_HOST)) ||
matchesHost(EXCLUDE_HOST) ||
isUnlockedByContentRestriction;

console.debug("ðŸ” Exclusion Result:", isExcluded ? "âœ… BLOCKED" : "âŒ NOT BLOCKED", {
matchedTags: matchesTag(EXCLUDE_TAGS),
matchedSections: matchesSection(EXCLUDE_SECTIONS),
matchedPaths: matchesPath(EXCLUDE_PATHS) && matchesHost(INCLUDE_HOST),
invalidHost: matchesHost(EXCLUDE_HOST),
restrictionCheck: isUnlockedByContentRestriction,
finalValue: isExcluded
});

if (isExcluded) {
console.debug("âŒ Paywall override BLOCKED due to exclusion rules.");
return 1;
}

// **Determine if URL is included**
const isIncluded = matchesTag(INCLUDE_TAGS) ||
matchesSection(INCLUDE_SECTIONS) ||
(matchesPath(INCLUDE_PATHS) && matchesHost(INCLUDE_HOST)) ||
isLockedByContentRestriction ||
publishedDuration >= publishedDurationThreshold;

console.debug("ðŸ” Inclusion Result:", isIncluded ? "âœ… ALLOWED" : "âŒ NOT ALLOWED", {
matchedTags: matchesTag(INCLUDE_TAGS),
matchedSections: matchesSection(INCLUDE_SECTIONS),
matchedPaths: matchesPath(INCLUDE_PATHS) && matchesHost(INCLUDE_HOST),
validHost: matchesHost(INCLUDE_HOST),
durationCheck: publishedDuration >= publishedDurationThreshold,
restrictionCheck: isLockedByContentRestriction,
finalValue: isIncluded
});

if (isIncluded) {
console.debug("âœ… Paywall override ALLOWED due to inclusion rules.");
return 2;
}

console.debug("âš ï¸ No rules matched. Defaulting to paywall enforcement.");
return 0;
}

function injectBlueConicPaywallEvent() {
console.debug("ðŸ”¹ Injecting BlueConic paywall event...");
try {
if (window.blueConicClient) {
const blueConicClientCheck = () => {
// prevent window potentially being accessed from SSR
if (typeof window !== "undefined") {
return typeof window.blueConicClient !== "undefined" && typeof window.blueConicClient.event !== "undefined" && typeof window.blueConicClient.event.subscribe !== "undefined";
}
return false;
};
const blueConicClientBindOnLoad = func => {
// prevent window potentially being accessed from SSR
if (typeof window !== "undefined") {
window.addEventListener("onBlueConicLoaded", func);
}
};
const blueConicClientOnLoad = action => blueConicClientCheck() ? action() : blueConicClientBindOnLoad(action);

blueConicClientOnLoad(() => {
window.blueConicClient.createEvent("premium_article_sophi_filtered");
console.debug("ðŸ”¹ Triggering BlueConic event");
});
} else {
console.warn("âš ï¸ BlueConic client is not available. Event not triggered.");
}
} catch (error) {
console.error("âŒ Error triggering BlueConic event:", error);
}
}

// Locate the Sophi SDK script in the document
const loader = document.querySelector("script#sophi-downloader");

const useSophiPaywall = async () => {
try {
if(window.keyValues?.pageType === "article") {
// Extract key values
const contentId =
window.keyValues?.articleId ||
window.keyValues?.sectionId ||
window.keyValues?.targetingSlice ||
"";
const sectionID = window.keyValues?.sectionId?.split("/")[1] || "";

// Initialize Sophi Paywall to gather information
window.sophi.paywall.init({
hostname: "www.dallasnews.com",
getContentId: async () => contentId,
getSection: async () => sectionID,
});

getUserStatus()
.then(async (user) => {

// Check if user is a subscriber.
// user.status: 0 (anonymous), 1 (registered), 2 (subscribed)
if (user.status === 2) {
console.debug("âœ… User is a subscriber. Skipping paywall.");
// No paywall for subscribers. Paywall-decision event not triggered.
return;
}

// Checking paywall override conditions
const paywallDecisionCode = shouldOverrideByRule(); // Returns 0, 1, or 2

let decisionSource = "";
let wallType = "";
let decisionResponse = null;
const modelInput = {
visitor: user.type, // no possible value for "subscribed" here as it is handled above
visit: await window.sophi.paywall.getVisitInformation(),
device: {
...await window.sophi.paywall.parseDeviceInformation(
navigator.userAgent
),
type: await getDeviceType(),
},
contentId,
section: sectionID,
};

console.debug("ðŸªµ getDecision Input:", modelInput);

// Call 'getDecision()' on every page, regardless of whether our rule has overridden the paywall.
// This ensures we track the data Sophi uses to make decisions, including cases influenced by our override rule.
console.debug("ðŸ”¹ Fetching paywall decision...");
decisionResponse = await window.sophi.paywall.getDecision(modelInput);

// Handle paywall decision based on 'paywallDecisionCode'
switch (paywallDecisionCode) {
case 0: // Default case: Call Sophi API for decision
decisionSource = "sophi";
if (decisionResponse?.wallType) {
wallType = decisionResponse?.wallType;
} else {
wallType = "no-wall";
console.error("âŒ No decision response received.");
}
break;
case 1: // Paywall override blocked by exclusion rules
decisionSource = "dmn";
wallType = "no-wall";
console.debug(
"ðŸš« Paywall enforcement: Access blocked by DMN exclusion rules (Code:",
paywallDecisionCode,
")."
);
break;
case 2: // Paywall override allowed by inclusion rules
decisionSource = "dmn";
wallType = "paywall";
console.debug(
"âœ… Paywall override determined by DMN rules (Code:",
paywallDecisionCode,
")."
);
break;
default:
decisionSource = "";
wallType = "paywall";
console.error("âŒ Invalid response from shouldOverrideByRule().");
}

console.debug("ðŸš€ Paywall Decision:", { decisionSource, wallType });

window.sophi.paywall.decisionSource = decisionSource;
window.sophi.paywall.bcListener = `${decisionSource}-${wallType}`; // Set BlueConic listener for paywall decision

if (wallType === "paywall") {
// Call function when window is ready
injectBlueConicPaywallEvent();
}

window.dataLayer.push({
event: "paywall-decision",
sophiInfo: { ...window.sophi.paywall.decision },
decisionSource,
wallType,
});
})
.catch((error) => {
console.error(error.message);
// Injections for paywall event
injectBlueConicPaywallEvent();
});
}
} catch (error) {
console.error("âš ï¸ Error during Sophi Paywall processing:", error);
// Injections for paywall event
injectBlueConicPaywallEvent();
}
};

loader.onload = useSophiPaywall;
loader.onerror = () =>
console.error("âŒ An error occurred while loading the Sophi SDK");

4.066c.017.002.032.012.05.012h13.454l-4.647-4.067z"></path></svg></a><a class="dmnc_social-icons-social-icons-module__rH-K0 relative border border-gray-medium flex whitespace-nowrap items-center p-3 mr-3 my-1 hover_bg-gray-light transition-all" href="javascript:window.print()" title="Print"><svg fill="currentColor" class="dmnc_social-icons-social-icons-module__-UxPq icon-inline " width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 15 15" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M13.125 2.813V0H1.875v2.813H0v5.624h1.875v2.813L5.625 15h7.5V8.437H15V2.814h-1.875zM11.25 13.124H6.562v-2.813H3.75v-3.75h7.5v6.563zm0-10.313h-7.5v-.937h7.5v.938z"></path></svg></a></div></div><div class="dmnc_features-trinity-ai-media-player-trinity-ai-module__XuKhb mb-4"><div class="trinity-tts-placeholder-icon-player"></div></div><div itemProp="articleBody" class="body-text dmnc_features-article-body-body-module__Ldbl- mb-8 false"><section><p class="body-text-paragraph">Justin Shafer was looking at up to 15 years in prison for allegedly harassing an FBI agent and federal judge with emails and social media posts.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">But on Thursday he walked out of the federal courthouse in Dallas, smiling and relieved that he is a free man, no longer facing the threat of prosecution.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__yDYG- flex items-center justify-center mb-6"><div id='b7904583-d8ef-46fc-b2a8-4d34d8b81779'></div></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer pleaded guilty to a lesser misdemeanor charge as part of an agreement with the government, just four days before his trial was set to begin. At the same Thursday hearing, he was sentenced to time he already served behind bars â€” about eight months â€” while awaiting trial.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer, 38, a computer technician from North Richland Hills, had faced four felony counts of<b style="font-size: 1em;"> </b>online stalking and a charge of violating a law that protects people who perform "certain official duties."</p><div class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__YgCAW md_pb-9 md_mb-7 md_pt-9 md_mt-7 pb-6 mb-9 px-9 w-full h-64 bg-blue-light border-t border-b border-gray-light pt-6 mt-9"><div class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__P1yIN inline-flex col-span-1 row-span-1 pb-4"><div class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__ByfdA flex-row"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 93.74 147.9" fill="currentColor" class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__11vBW md_w-10 w-9 mr-6"><path d="M93.74 106.9c-11.2 5.9-20.8 13.6-29.1 23.2-7.7-6.8-17.5-10.3-27.6-9.7-18 0-26.7 4.4-26.7 13.1 0 3.5 1.5 6.3 4.4 8.3 2.4 2 5.9 3.5 9.2 3.5 3.5 0 6.3-.9 8.8-2.9l-.5 3.5c-2.9 1.5-6.3 2-9.2 2-4.8 0-9.7-1.5-13.6-4.8-4.4-3.5-6.3-9.2-6.3-14.6 0-8.3 4.8-15.5 11.6-19.5 8.8-4.8 19-7.2 29.1-6.8V26.8c-4.8.9-9.7 1.5-14.6 1.5-7.8.4-15.6-1.5-22.4-5.3-4.8-4.4-7.2-10.7-6.8-17.1 0-.5.5-2.4.9-5.9h.9c.9 3.5 2.9 6.3 5.9 8.3 5.3 2.4 10.7 3.5 16.4 2.9 6.8-.5 13.6-.9 20.4-2.4s13.1-2.4 19.9-2.9c19.5 0 29.1 10.7 29.1 32l.2 69m-52.8-74.8c-3.5 2.9-5.3 7.7-4.8 12.1v35c0 12.1-8.8 21.4-25.8 26.7l-1.5-1.5c5.3-2.9 8.8-8.8 7.7-15.1V74.2h-3.5c-4.4-.9-8.8 2-9.7 6.3h-.5c-1.5-2.4-2-4.8-2-7.7-.9-6.3 3.5-12.7 9.7-13.1h5.9V52c0-11.2 7.7-18.4 22.8-21.4l1.7 1.5zm31.5 25.3v-17c.5-4.4-.9-8.8-2.9-12.1-2.4-2.9-6.3-3.9-9.7-3.9-4.4.5-9.2.9-13.6 2v31.1c4.4.9 8.3 2 12.7 2 4.8-.1 9.1-1.2 13.5-2.1zm0 16.4V59.2c-4.4 1.5-8.8 2-13.1 2s-8.8-.5-12.7-2v14.6c4.4-1.5 8.3-2 12.7-2 4.4.1 8.7.5 13.1 2zm0 37v-35c-4.4-.9-8.8-2-13.1-2s-8.8.5-12.7 2v26.3c9.2.4 18 3.3 25.8 8.7z"></path></svg></div><div class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__vRSrF flex-auto w-full"><div class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__3hNhh primaryBold primaryBold-50 mb-3">Crime in The News</div><p class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__zWZy- mb-4">Read the crime and public safety news your neighbors are talking about.</p></div></div><div class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__EM6J4 col-span-1 row-span-1"><div class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__8z1aU md_flex md_flex-row md_flex-nowrap gap-x-5"><div xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 19.6 20" class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__IZDL4 dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__Fa1DT md_align-middle mr-4 h-min w-6 class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__8zeU5 inline-flex secondaryBoldCaps secondaryBoldCaps-20 cursor-pointer border rounded-sm md_ml-6 md_mr-0 md_p-4 md_my-0 link-hover-blue hover_border-blue hover_outline hover_outline-blue mr-3 py-3 px-1 my-2 text-center align-middle"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 500 498.17" fill="currentColor" class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__C4F4n dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__Fa1DT md_align-middle mr-4 h-min w-6 align-text-top inline-flex text-facebook"><path d="M250 0C111.93 0 0 111.93 0 250c0 117.24 80.72 215.62 189.61 242.64V326.4h-51.55V250h51.55v-32.92c0-85.09 38.51-124.53 122.05-124.53 15.84 0 43.17 3.11 54.35 6.21v69.25c-5.9-.62-16.15-.93-28.88-.93-40.99 0-56.83 15.53-56.83 55.9V250h81.66l-14.03 76.4H280.3v171.77C404.09 483.22 500.01 377.82 500.01 250 500 111.93 388.07 0 250 0z"></path></svg>Facebook</div></div></div><p class="dmnc_features-cta-social-cta-social-module__M0cTf flex flex-wrap py-4 text-gray-dark secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-15 contains-link-blue-dark-underline">By signing up you agree to our <a href="/help/terms-of-service/">Terms of Service</a> and <a href="/help/privacy-policy">Privacy Policy</a></p></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Prosecutors previously argued that he harassed the FBI agent who was investigating him for computer hacking, as retaliation. Shafer countered that his actions were protected speech. Under Thursday's agreement, Shafer admitted to committing simple assault by sending intimidating messages on social media to the agent's wife.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer's attorney, <a href="https://torekeland.com/" style="font-size: 1em;">Tor Ekeland</a>, a New York-based computer law specialist, said the favorable plea agreement came about after a federal judge recently expressed skepticism about the prosecutors' case.<p class="line-break"></p></p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__D24FM w-full mb-6 htlad-nativeArticleInline" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/nativeArticleInline" data-targeting="{&quot;native&quot;:&quot;nativeArticleInline&quot;,&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;1&quot;}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Legal arguments in the trial would have added to a growing debate about a form of online harassment known as doxing that is testing the limits of free speech.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Doxing">Doxing</a>, which Shafer was accused of, occurs when someone posts a person's personal information online such as a home address, email address and place of employment. But it is not illegal unless someone makes clear and specific threats or does it while stalking the victim.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">However, some have called for new laws addressing "malicious doxing." In June, a bill was introduced in Congress that would have criminalized doxing in some forms.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6 md_hidden"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__YIHSg dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__u4HRm dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 md_hidden htlad-dfpPosition2_article" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition2_article" data-targeting="{}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer had been accused of causing "substantial emotional distress" to the FBI agent and his wife by making "derogatory and inflammatory statements" about him on Twitter and posting identifying information about his wife and other family members.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6 hidden md_flex"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__-zD5N flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-desktopInline2" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/desktopInline2" data-targeting="{}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Senior Judge Janis Graham Jack, from the Southern District of Texas, accepted the plea agreement Thursday. The U.S. attorney's office in Dallas and the judge initially assigned to the case recused themselves.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer did not make a statement during the speedy hearing. Under the plea, he also agreed not to contact the agent or his family or the Dallas judge and his staff. No fine or restitution was ordered.</p><div class=""><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__aJKMz hidden">Advertisement</div><div class="" id="teads-article-ad"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer's case generated interest in computer tech circles, which were abuzz with speculation about whether the FBI unfairly targeted him with stalking charges because agents could not make an illegal-hacking case.</p><figure class="align-left"><img loading="lazy" style="aspect-ratio:769 / 1024" sizes="(min-width: 1300px) 403px, (min-width: 768px) 30vw, 50vw" srcSet="https://dmn-dallas-news-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/LOKZVSEG77UUH5IN4EJUK6EDTU.jpg?auth=0f1f1314ea5eef8a5c4b27187b0cd7a48600ce3fe519be8f3b17012d779fed36&amp;width=430&amp;quality=80 430w, https://dmn-dallas-news-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/LOKZVSEG77UUH5IN4EJUK6EDTU.jpg?auth=0f1f1314ea5eef8a5c4b27187b0cd7a48600ce3fe519be8f3b17012d779fed36&amp;width=830&amp;quality=80 830w" class="dmnc_images-modern-image-module__QFaG- max-w-full h-auto text-white dmnc_images-modern-image-module__9Zlll bg-gray-light object-contain" width="769" height="1024" src="https://dmn-dallas-news-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/LOKZVSEG77UUH5IN4EJUK6EDTU.jpg?auth=0f1f1314ea5eef8a5c4b27187b0cd7a48600ce3fe519be8f3b17012d779fed36&amp;width=430&amp;quality=80" alt="Justin Shafer"/><figcaption class="dmnc_images-image-elements-module__ku669 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-10 mt-3 text-gray-medium">Justin Shafer<span class="dmnc_images-image-elements-module__7oO0P pl-1">(N/A)</span></figcaption></figure><p class="body-text-paragraph">Ekeland said he took the case at a heavily discounted rate because it was such an egregious affront to the First Amendment. He said his client never made any direct or implied threats against the agent or his wife, and he didn't call for others to harass or harm them.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">"If what he did was cyberstalking, they can go after almost anybody," Ekeland said.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__Z-JdA dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-dfpPosition" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition" data-targeting="{&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;1&quot;}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">He filed a motion in January to dismiss the indictment, arguing that his client's social media posts are protected by the First Amendment, and he blasted the government for an "outrageous prosecution."</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer, he said, merely wanted government officials to return his seized computers, which included family photos. But they ignored his inquiries, Ekeland said. Agents seized the items as part of their hacking investigation.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Assistant U.S. Attorney Douglas W. Gardner said in a previous court filing that Shafer "engaged in a barrage of harassing and intimidating actions."</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">He said the agent's wife obtained a firearm, lived somewhere "else for a time" and took other security measures out of concern over Shafer's "increasingly belligerent" actions.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__Z-JdA dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-dfpPosition" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition" data-targeting="{&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;2&quot;}"></div></div><h2 class="body-text-header">Emotional distress</h2><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer was arrested in March 2017 for posting about the agent and his wife on social media, which prosecutors say constituted harassment.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">The agent was investigating him for the alleged hacking of medical patient data. Agents also suspected Shafer was associated with a notorious computer hacker or hacking group called <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/answer-sheet/wp/2017/10/26/education-department-warns-of-new-hacker-threat-as-dark-overlord-claims-credit-for-attacks-on-school-districts/?utm_term=.ff4450fb9e59">TheDarkOverlord</a>.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">The government updated the indictment earlier this month to add a stalking charge for the voluminous emails Shafer sent to the magistrate judge who signed the FBI warrants authorizing two separate searches of his home.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__Z-JdA dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-dfpPosition" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition" data-targeting="{&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;3&quot;}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer contacted U.S. Magistrate Judge Jeffrey Cureton about his seized property and was ignored, Ekeland said.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">"Everything in this case returns to Mr. Shafer typing at his keyboard seeking redress for his grievances from an unresponsive government," Ekeland said in his motion to dismiss.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Prosecutors previously said Shafer sent "hundreds of emails with attachments" to Cureton's government email address. "Some of the language in the emails was concerning and caused substantial emotional distress," prosecutors said in a court filing. They said the judge and his staff were concerned about the emails.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__Z-JdA dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-dfpPosition" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition" data-targeting="{&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;4&quot;}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">The sometimes insulting tweets and Facebook posts in question were posted from May 2016 through March 2017. Shafer posted a past home address for the agent as well as Facebook profiles of his mother, cousin, wife and ex-wife. Shafer also sent a Facebook friend request to the agent's wife and messaged her on Facebook, according to the FBI.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">And Shafer followed the agent's wife on Twitter "in an attempt to harass and intimidate her," court records said.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Case law exists that protects crude and abusive tweets directed at another person. A federal district court in Maryland dismissed an indictment against a man in 2011 who was accused of causing a Buddhist religious leader emotional distress with his blogs and tweets about her.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">In his tweets, the defendant told the victim to kill herself, among other things. But the judge ruled that the First Amendment protects "uncomfortable" speech online and that none of the tweets were "true threats." The judge also said the tweets and blog posts were similar to a physical bulletin board where recipients of unkind messages could simply ignore them.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__Z-JdA dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-dfpPosition" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition" data-targeting="{&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;5&quot;}"></div></div><h2 class="body-text-header">Internet vigilante?</h2><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer runs a business that does computer work for dental offices. On the side, he is a computer security professional, his lawyer says.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">The FBI raided Shafer's house in January 2017 and found a database of about 48,000 records on his computer that TheDarkOverlord was selling, the FBI affidavit said.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer said on his blog that he notified the FBI the year before that the hackers had shared their stolen records with him and he sent the bureau a copy of the database.</p><figure class="align-left"><img loading="lazy" style="aspect-ratio:644 / 295" sizes="(min-width: 1300px) 403px, (min-width: 768px) 30vw, 50vw" srcSet="https://dmn-dallas-news-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/Z3RP2MUJT3FH4VLK4A3TLDF5OM.jpg?auth=5327debbe4a20ac79f212e9638f51d322fbd423dc9a7d2f78ccfcff2e164ae2a&amp;width=430&amp;quality=80 430w, https://dmn-dallas-news-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/Z3RP2MUJT3FH4VLK4A3TLDF5OM.jpg?auth=5327debbe4a20ac79f212e9638f51d322fbd423dc9a7d2f78ccfcff2e164ae2a&amp;width=830&amp;quality=80 830w" class="dmnc_images-modern-image-module__QFaG- max-w-full h-auto text-white dmnc_images-modern-image-module__9Zlll bg-gray-light object-contain" width="644" height="295" src="https://dmn-dallas-news-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/v2/Z3RP2MUJT3FH4VLK4A3TLDF5OM.jpg?auth=5327debbe4a20ac79f212e9638f51d322fbd423dc9a7d2f78ccfcff2e164ae2a&amp;width=430&amp;quality=80" alt="A Justin Shafer tweet to the FBI."/><figcaption class="dmnc_images-image-elements-module__ku669 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-10 mt-3 text-gray-medium">A Justin Shafer tweet to the FBI.<span class="dmnc_images-image-elements-module__7oO0P pl-1">(Twitter)</span></figcaption></figure><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer says he searches the internet for public, unsecured computer servers that store confidential patient medical information.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">He says he tries to access data and then alerts companies that own the data that it is not secured. He documents his findings as well as his communications with the companies on his blog and Twitter account, sometimes posting screenshots.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__Z-JdA dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-dfpPosition" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition" data-targeting="{&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;6&quot;}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">Shafer also has reported his findings to federal agencies and news websites. Companies can be fined by the government for using outdated and unsecured technology to store protected data.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">"Rather than reward Mr. Shafer for his efforts to make the internet safer, the FBI chose to engage in armed raid of his family home," Ekeland said in his motion to dismiss the charges.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Prosecutors previously called Shafer a "self-styled internet vigilante" who goes beyond merely reporting security breaches and instead improperly downloads the personal information of numerous medical patients.</p><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__cOFTB flex flex-col items-center dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__ffux4 border-t border-b border-gray-light mb-6"><div class="dmnc_features-ads-arc-ad-_children-ad-wrapper-module__3Ge73 uppercase py-4 secondaryRoman secondaryRoman-9 text-gray-dark">Advertisement</div><div class="dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__Z-JdA dmnc_features-ads-config-presets-module__N2M5T flex items-center justify-center mb-6 htlad-dfpPosition" data-unit="dmn/news/crime/article/dfpPosition" data-targeting="{&quot;scroll&quot;:&quot;7&quot;}"></div></div><p class="body-text-paragraph">On Thursday, Gardner told the judge that prosecutors in Dallas have agreed not to prosecute Shafer over the hacking allegations in the search warrant.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">Ekeland said Americans have a First Amendment right to talk to the government, especially during a criminal prosecution.</p><p class="body-text-paragraph">"He asked for an answer and he got silence. And he kept on asking, and all he got was silence. And eventually he is charged with a crime," he said. "It's really, really dangerous what they did here."</p></section></div><div class="hidden">ex.co script has been added to the page</div><div class="dmnc_generic-share-bar-share-bar-module__C7Mzo flex window.courierEndpoint = 'https://courier-api.dallasnews.com' || [];

const showLoginFrame = function (event) {
const targets = ['courier-login', 'newsletter-login'];
if (typeof event.target.id !== "undefined") {
if (!targets.includes(event.target.id)) {
document.removeEventListener('click', showLoginFrame, false);
hideLogin();
}
}
}

window.showLogin = function() {
event.stopPropagation();
window.loginOpen = true;
document.getElementById('courier-login').style.display='block';
document.getElementById('courier-login-iframe').src = 'https://www.dallasnews.com/login/';
document.addEventListener('click', showLoginFrame, false);
};

window.showVfLogin = function() {
window.loginOpen = true;
document.getElementById('courier-login').style.display='block';
document.getElementById('courier-login-iframe').src = 'https://www.dallasnews.com/login-v2/';
document.addEventListener('click', showLoginFrame, false);
};

window.hideLogin = function() {
window.loginOpen = false;
document.getElementById('courier-login').style.display='none';
document.getElementById('courier-login-iframe').src = '';
};

function getCookie(name) {
const startIndex = document.cookie.indexOf(name + "=");
if (startIndex !== -1) {
var endIndex = document.cookie.indexOf(";", startIndex + 1);
const cookieValueIndex = startIndex + name.length + 1;
if(endIndex === -1) {
endIndex = document.cookie.length;
}
return document.cookie.substring(cookieValueIndex, endIndex);
}
return null;
}

function setCookie(name, value, days, rootDomain) {
rootDomain = (rootDomain === undefined ? false : rootDomain);
var expires = "";
if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
expires = ";expires=" + date.toUTCString();
}

var c = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
if (rootDomain) {
c += "; domain=." + window.location.hostname.split('.').slice(-2).join('.');
}
document.cookie = c;
}

function triggerEvent(name, data) {
var event;
if (window.CustomEvent) {
event = new CustomEvent(name, { detail: data });
} else {
event = document.createEvent('CustomEvent');
event.initCustomEvent(name, true, true, { detail: data });
}
document.dispatchEvent(event);
}

function planToMatherOffer(plan) {
if (!plan || !("detail" in plan)) return;

var r = plan.detail.planIntervalUnit.match(/(.*)s$/); // strip off plurality from unit
var interval = (r && typeof r[1] !== "undefined") ? r[1] : plan.detail.planIntervalUnit;
return {
offerId: plan.code,
offerName: plan.detail.name,
price: plan.detail.amount,
per: interval,
termAmount: plan.detail.planIntervalLength,
termUnit: interval,
};
}

window.addEventListener("message", function(event) {
if (typeof event.data == "object" && "command" in event.data) {
const loginFrame = document.getElementById('courier-login-iframe');
const staticFrame = document.getElementById('courier-static-offers');
const dynamicFrame = document.getElementById('courier-arc-offers');

const courierDiv = document.getElementById('courier-iframe');
const courierDivFrame = courierDiv && courierDiv.iframe;

const theFrame = staticFrame || dynamicFrame || courierDivFrame || loginFrame;

switch (event.data.command) {
case "set-entitlements":
console.log('arc: setting entitlements');
window._matherq.push(['paywallEvent', { category: 'payment', action: 'logon' }, null]);
window.initBC(event.data.value, function() {
window.location.reload(true);
});
break;

case "size-change":
if (theFrame) {
theFrame.style.height = event.data.height + 'px';
} else {
console.warn("arc: !size-change");
}
break;

case "sow":
switch (event.data.key) {
case "DMN-P":
setCookie(event.data.key, event.data.value, event.data.expire, true);
break;
default:
setCookie(event.data.key, event.data.value, event.data.expire);
break;
}
break;

case "select-plan":
const plans = event.data.plan || {};
window._matherq.push(['paywallEvent', {
category: 'payment',
action: 'subscription_selected',
offers: [this.planToMatherOffer(event.data.plan)]
}, null]);
window._matherq.push(['paywallEvent', { category: 'payment', action: 'address_information' }, null]);
window._matherq.push(['paywallEvent', { category: 'payment', action: 'payment_information' }, null]);
//Set dataLayer event
window.dataLayer.push({ event: 'meterEvent', action: 'select-plan', category: 'Courier_Subscribe',
offers: [this.planToMatherOffer(event.data.plan)] });
break;

case "terms-shown":
window._matherq.push(['paywallEvent', { category: 'payment', action: 'terms_and_conditions' }, null]);
break;

case "account-purchase":
const purchase = typeof event.data.purchase !== 'undefined' ? event.data.purchase : null;
dataLayer.push(purchase.pevent);
window._matherq.push(['paywallEvent', { category: 'payment', action: 'completed' }, null]);
dataLayer.push({'event': 'courier/convert'});
break;
}
}
}.bind(this), false);
